  \begin{scope}[

    { 
    	\nodepart{one} 
    	\nodepart{two} 
    	\nodepart{three}
    	\nodepart{four}0x00000023
    	\nodepart{five}0x00000310 
    	\nodepart{six}0xFFFFFF01 
    	\nodepart{seven}0x00009801
    	\nodepart{eight}0xFFFFC024 
    	\nodepart{nine}0x00000030 
    	\nodepart{ten}
    };
  \end{scope}

  \node at (0.5,3.05) {i [0]};
  \node at (0.5,2.7) {i [1]};
  \node at (0.5,2.35) {i [2]};
  \node at (0.5,2.05) {i [3]};
  \node at (0.5,1.7) {i [4]};
  \node at (0.5,1.4) {i [5]};
  \node at (3.8,3.05) {0x3F0048\textcolor{red}{00}};
  \node at (3.8,2.7) {0x3Ff0048\textcolor{red}{04}};
  \node at (3.8,2.35) {0x3F0048\textcolor{red}{08}};
  \node at (3.8,2.05) {0x3F0048\textcolor{red}{0C}};
  \node at (3.8,1.7) {0x3F0048\textcolor{red}{10}};
  \node at (3.8,1.4) {0x3F0048\textcolor{red}{14}};
  \node at (0.2,4.8) {Elementos de};
  \node at (0.2,4.6) {la variable};
  \node at (3.9,4.8) {Dirección};
  \node at (2.1,4.8) {Contenido};
  \node at (2.1,6.5) {\normalsize Declaración en código};
  \node at (2.1,6.0) {\normalsize \textcolor{blue}{int c[6]}  };
  \draw[->] ($(R.north)+(1.8,10pt)$) to [out=-90,in=90]node[right,midway]{} ++(0,-1.2) ; 
  \draw[->] ($(R.north)+(-1.9,0pt)$) to [out=-90,in=90]node[right,midway]{} ++(0.3,-0.8) ; 
  \draw[->] ($(R.north)+(0,10pt)$) to [out=-90,in=90]node[right,midway]{} ++(0,-1.2) ; 
  \draw[decorate,decoration={brace,raise=6pt,amplitude=8pt}, thick]
    (3,1) -- (1.2,1)node [black,midway,xshift=0.0cm,yshift=-0.7cm]{\footnotesize $4$ $bytes$};
\end{tikzpicture}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

\begin{frame}[fragile]
 \frametitle{Un caso especial de arreglo}
  \begin{block}{Arreglo de caracteres}
Se trata de un tipo muy usual de dato que llamamos cadena o string (del inglés). \\
Se inicializa de los siguientes modos:
  \end{block}
\pause
  \lstset{basicstyle=\scriptsize}
  \lstset{backgroundcolor=\color{gray!20}}
     \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
/*Una forma de inicializar un areglo de caracteres con una cadena*/

char cad []= "Hola mundo!";

/* Otra forma...*/

char cad []={'H','o','l','a',' ','m','u','n','d','o','!','\0'};
\end{lstlisting}
\end{frame}

\begin{frame}[fragile]
 \frametitle{En código....}
  \lstset{basicstyle=\small}
  \lstset{backgroundcolor=\color{gray!20}}
     \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
  /* Utiliza una lista de inicialización para inicializar el arreglo arr.*/
  int arr[8] = {23,0,-669,-1,995,1277,90,-9000};
  /* La cantidad de elementos en la línea anterior es redundante. Puede hacerse lo mismo de la siguiente forma*/
  int arr[] = {23,0,-669,-1,995,1277,90,-9000};
  /*Si lo vamos a inicializar con el mismo valor para todos los elementos, la forma adecuada es la siguiente*/

  int arr[8], i;
  for (i = 0 ; i < 8 ; i++)
  {  
  	arr[i] = 0;
  }
\end{lstlisting}
\end{frame}

  \node at (0,0.5) {\tiny \color{cyan}0x7FFE6E23};
  \node at (0,0.05) {\tiny \color{cyan}0x7FFE6E27};
  \node at (0,-0.35) {\tiny \color{cyan}0x7FFE6E2B};
  \node at (0,-0.8) {\tiny \color{cyan}0x7FFE6E2F};
  \node at (0,-2) {\tiny \color{cyan}0xFFFFFFFF};
  \node at (4.3,-2) {\tiny \color{cyan}0xFFFFFFC};
\end{tikzpicture}
  \column{3.9\textwidth}
  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
  \vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};

  \column{3.9\textwidth}
  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
  \vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;

  {
    resto++;

        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);

   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
  \vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

  \vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
  \vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}

   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  resto=0;
  do
  {
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++)
    {
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1])
      {
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
return (0);
}

  \column{3.9\textwidth}
  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

void imprimir(int *p,int n);

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  resto=0;
  do{
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++){
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1]){
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}
void imprimir( int*p,int n)
{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));
  }
}


   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}

        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}

{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));

{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  resto=0;
  do{
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++){
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1]){
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}
void imprimir( int*p,int n)
{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));
  }
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}

      (10.8,3.3) -- (5.6,3.3) -- (5.6,3.0) -- (10.8,3.0) -- cycle;

      (10.8,-0.1) -- (5.6,-0.1) -- (5.6,-0.4) -- (10.8,-0.4) -- cycle;

  \draw[red,dashed,->](7.6,-1.6)to [out=150,in=0]node[right,midway]{} ++(-3.7,0.6) ; 


\end{tikzpicture}
  \column{3.9\textwidth}
  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

void imprimir(int *p,int n);

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  resto=0;
  do{
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++){
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1]){
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}
void imprimir( int*p,int n)
{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));
  }
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

void imprimir(int *p,int n);

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  resto=0;
  do{
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++){
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1]){
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}
void imprimir( int*p,int n)
{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));
  }
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

void imprimir(int *p,int n);

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  resto=0;
  do{
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++){
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1]){
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}
void imprimir( int*p,int n)
{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));
  }
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

  \draw[red,dashed,->](8.7,-1.95)to [out=90,in=-20]node[right,midway]{} ++(-4.9,2.2) ;

  \column{3.9\textwidth}
  \lstset{basicstyle=\tiny}
\vspace{-0.5cm}
   \begin{lstlisting}[escapechar=\|,label=noint]
#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

void imprimir(int *p,int n);

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  resto=0;
  do{
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++){
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1]){
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}
void imprimir( int*p,int n)
{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));
  }
}
   \end{lstlisting}
 \end{columns}
\end{frame}

#include <stdio.h>
#define CANT		6

void imprimir(int *p,int n);

int main (void)
{
int aux,resto,i,flag,vInt[CANT]={2,286,9,59,928,3};
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  resto=0;
  do{
    resto++;
    flag=0;
    for(i=0;i < (CANT-resto);i++){
      if(vInt[i] > vInt[i+1]){
        aux=vInt[i];
        vInt[i]=vInt[i+1];
        vInt[i+1]=aux;
        flag=1;
      }
    }  
  }while(flag);
  imprimir(&vInt[0],CANT);
  return (0);
}
void imprimir( int*p,int n)
{
  int j;
  for(j=0;j<n;j++){
   printf("% d \r\n",*(p+j));
  }
}

\begin{frame}
\begin{center}
	  {\includegraphics[scale=0.7]{print-burbuja.png}};
\end{center}
\begin{itemize}
\item compila con \textbf{\textit{\color{red}gcc -c burbuja.c -o burbuja.o -Wall}} 
\item Linkea con \textbf{\textit{\color{red}gcc  burbuja.o -o burbuja -Wall}}
\item Ejecuta con \textbf{\textit{\color{red}./burbuja}}
\item Primero imprime en la consola los valores desordenados
\item Al finalizar el ordenamiento también los imprime en la consola

\end{itemize}
\end{frame}
